## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Rust ICE in Trait Method Candidate Collection

## Your Task

Users report an internal compiler error (ICE) during trait method resolution. Find the Rust source files in rust-lang/rust that (1) collect candidate trait method implementations and (2) report ambiguous trait method errors.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the incident domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/rust--01f6ddf7, sg-evals/servo--be6a2f99.

## Summary

I identified the key Rust source files involved in trait method candidate collection and ambiguous trait method error reporting:

### 1. `compiler/rustc_hir_typeck/src/method/probe.rs` — Candidate Collection
This is the primary file for collecting trait method implementation candidates. It contains:
- **`ProbeContext`** struct with `inherent_candidates` and `extension_candidates` vectors
- **`CandidateKind`** enum: `InherentImplCandidate`, `ObjectCandidate`, `TraitCandidate`, `WhereClauseCandidate`
- Assembly functions: `assemble_inherent_candidates()`, `assemble_probe()`, `assemble_inherent_impl_probe()`, `assemble_inherent_candidates_from_object()`, `assemble_inherent_candidates_from_param()`, `assemble_candidates_for_bounds()`, `assemble_extension_candidates_for_traits_in_scope()`, `assemble_extension_candidates_for_all_traits()`, `assemble_extension_candidates_for_trait()`
- **`consider_candidates()`** — returns `MethodError::Ambiguity` when multiple candidates match
- **`pick()` / `pick_core()`** — drive the overall resolution

### 2. `compiler/rustc_hir_typeck/src/method/suggest.rs` — Ambiguity Error Reporting
- **`report_method_error()`** — handles `MethodError::Ambiguity` and emits E0034 "multiple applicable items in scope"
- **`note_candidates_on_method_error()`** — lists each ambiguous candidate in the error output

### 3. `compiler/rustc_hir_typeck/src/method/mod.rs` — Supporting Types
- **`MethodError::Ambiguity(Vec<CandidateSource>)`** — the error variant for multiple applicable methods
- **`CandidateSource`** — distinguishes `Impl` vs `Trait` sources
